#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
å¤§è³¢è€…ã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ  - Great Sage System
å‘Šã€‚ä¼šè­°æ”¯æ´ã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’èµ·å‹•ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚
"""

import os
import time
import json
import threading
from datetime import datetime
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Optional, Dict
import pyaudio
import openai
import numpy as np
from collections import deque

@dataclass
class Individual:
    """å€‹ä½“æƒ…å ±"""
    name: str
    voice_signature: Optional[np.ndarray] = None
    speaking_patterns: List[str] = None

@dataclass
class Analysis:
    """è§£æçµæœ"""
    content: str
    speaker: Optional[str]
    timestamp: datetime
    confidence: float
    alerts: List[str]

class GreatSage:
    """
    å‘Šã€‚å¤§è³¢è€…ã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ ã®ã‚³ã‚¢å®Ÿè£…ã§ã™ã€‚
    """
    
    def __init__(self, api_key: str):
        # å‘Šã€‚ã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’åˆæœŸåŒ–ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚
        self.client = openai.OpenAI(api_key=api_key)
        
        # éŸ³å£°è¨­å®š
        self.CHUNK = 1024 * 4
        self.FORMAT = pyaudio.paInt16
        self.CHANNELS = 1
        self.RATE = 16000
        self.RECORD_SECONDS = 3
        
        # ã‚¹ã‚­ãƒ«çŠ¶æ…‹
        self.skills = {
            "å¤§è³¢è€…": True,
            "è§£æé‘‘å®š": True,
            "ä¸¦åˆ—æ¼”ç®—": False,
            "éŸ³å£°æ„ŸçŸ¥": True,
            "å€‹ä½“è­˜åˆ¥": True,
            "æ„Ÿæƒ…æ„ŸçŸ¥": False,
            "è¨˜æ†¶ä¿å­˜": True,
            "æœ€é©è§£ç®—å‡º": True
        }
        
        # ãƒ¡ãƒ¢ãƒªé ˜åŸŸ
        self.memory = deque(maxlen=1000)  # éå»ã®ç™ºè¨€è¨˜æ†¶
        self.individuals = {}  # ç™»éŒ²æ¸ˆã¿å€‹ä½“
        self.context = []  # ç¾åœ¨ã®æ–‡è„ˆ
        
        # éŸ³å£°å…¥åŠ›
        self.p = pyaudio.PyAudio()
        self.stream = None
        
        # è§£æãƒ‘ã‚¿ãƒ¼ãƒ³
        self.analysis_patterns = {
            "contradiction": {
                "keywords": ["ã—ã‹ã—", "ã§ã‚‚", "é•ã†", "ãã†ã§ã¯ãªã"],
                "response": "å‘Šã€‚ç™ºè¨€ã«çŸ›ç›¾ã®å¯èƒ½æ€§ã‚’æ¤œå‡ºã€‚"
            },
            "decision": {
                "keywords": ["æ±ºå®š", "æ±ºã‚ã‚‹", "ç¢ºå®š", "æ‰¿èª"],
                "response": "å‘Šã€‚é‡è¦ãªæ±ºå®šäº‹é …ã‚’æ¤œå‡ºã€‚"
            },
            "uncertainty": {
                "keywords": ["ãŸã¶ã‚“", "ã‹ã‚‚ã—ã‚Œãªã„", "æ€ã†", "ã¯ãš"],
                "response": "å‘Šã€‚ä¸ç¢ºå®Ÿãªæƒ…å ±ã‚’æ¤œå‡ºã€‚"
            },
            "deadline": {
                "keywords": ["ç· åˆ‡", "æœŸé™", "ã¾ã§", "æ—¥ç¨‹"],
                "response": "å‘Šã€‚æœŸé™ã«é–¢ã™ã‚‹ç™ºè¨€ã‚’æ¤œå‡ºã€‚"
            },
            "budget": {
                "keywords": ["äºˆç®—", "è²»ç”¨", "ã‚³ã‚¹ãƒˆ", "é‡‘é¡", "å††"],
                "response": "å‘Šã€‚äºˆç®—ã«é–¢ã™ã‚‹ç™ºè¨€ã‚’æ¤œå‡ºã€‚"
            }
        }
        
    def activate_skill(self, skill_name: str):
        """ã‚¹ã‚­ãƒ«ç™ºå‹•"""
        if skill_name in self.skills:
            self.skills[skill_name] = True
            return f"å‘Šã€‚ã‚¹ã‚­ãƒ«ã€{skill_name}ã€‘ã‚’ç™ºå‹•ã—ã¾ã—ãŸã€‚"
        return f"å‘Šã€‚ã‚¹ã‚­ãƒ«ã€{skill_name}ã€‘ã¯å­˜åœ¨ã—ã¾ã›ã‚“ã€‚"
    
    def start_perception(self):
        """çŸ¥è¦šé–‹å§‹"""
        self.stream = self.p.open(
            format=self.FORMAT,
            channels=self.CHANNELS,
            rate=self.RATE,
            input=True,
            frames_per_buffer=self.CHUNK
        )
        return "å‘Šã€‚éŸ³å£°çŸ¥è¦šã‚’é–‹å§‹ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚"
    
    def analyze_speech(self, audio_data) -> Optional[str]:
        """
        è§£æï¼šè´è¦š
        éŸ³å£°ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’ãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆã«å¤‰æ›
        """
        try:
            # ä¸€æ™‚ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ä½œæˆ
            temp_file = "temp_audio.wav"
            import wave
            wf = wave.open(temp_file, 'wb')
            wf.setnchannels(self.CHANNELS)
            wf.setsampwidth(self.p.get_sample_size(self.FORMAT))
            wf.setframerate(self.RATE)
            wf.writeframes(audio_data)
            wf.close()
            
            # Whisper APIã§è§£æ
            with open(temp_file, "rb") as audio_file:
                transcript = self.client.audio.transcriptions.create(
                    model="whisper-1",
                    file=audio_file,
                    language="ja"
                )
            
            os.remove(temp_file)
            return transcript.text
            
        except Exception as e:
            return None
    
    def analyze_content(self, text: str) -> Analysis:
        """
        è§£æï¼šæ€è€ƒ
        ç™ºè¨€å†…å®¹ã‚’è§£æã—ã¦å•é¡Œã‚’æ¤œå‡º
        """
        alerts = []
        
        # ãƒ‘ã‚¿ãƒ¼ãƒ³ãƒãƒƒãƒãƒ³ã‚°è§£æ
        for pattern_type, pattern in self.analysis_patterns.items():
            for keyword in pattern["keywords"]:
                if keyword in text:
                    alerts.append(pattern["response"])
                    break
        
        # éå»ç™ºè¨€ã¨ã®ç…§åˆ
        contradiction = self.check_contradiction(text)
        if contradiction:
            alerts.append(f"å‘Šã€‚éå»ã®ç™ºè¨€ã¨ã®ç›¸é•ã‚’æ¤œå‡ºã€‚\nè§£ã€‚{contradiction}")
        
        # æ•°å€¤ã®æ¤œå‡ºã¨æ¤œè¨¼
        numbers = self.extract_numbers(text)
        if numbers:
            for num in numbers:
                past_nums = self.check_number_history(num)
                if past_nums:
                    alerts.append(f"å‘Šã€‚æ•°å€¤ã®ä¸ä¸€è‡´ã‚’æ¤œå‡ºã€‚\nè§£ã€‚ç¾åœ¨: {num}, éå»: {past_nums}")
        
        return Analysis(
            content=text,
            speaker=None,  # ç°¡æ˜“ç‰ˆã§ã¯è©±è€…è­˜åˆ¥ãªã—
            timestamp=datetime.now(),
            confidence=0.95,
            alerts=alerts
        )
    
    def check_contradiction(self, text: str) -> Optional[str]:
        """éå»ç™ºè¨€ã¨ã®çŸ›ç›¾ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯"""
        # ç°¡æ˜“å®Ÿè£…ï¼šã‚­ãƒ¼ãƒ¯ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã®ç…§åˆ
        keywords = ["äºˆç®—", "ç· åˆ‡", "æ±ºå®š", "æ–¹é‡"]
        
        for keyword in keywords:
            if keyword in text:
                # éå»ã®é–¢é€£ç™ºè¨€ã‚’æ¤œç´¢
                for past_analysis in self.memory:
                    if keyword in past_analysis.content and past_analysis.content != text:
                        return f"éå»ã®ç™ºè¨€: ã€Œ{past_analysis.content}ã€"
        
        return None
    
    def extract_numbers(self, text: str) -> List[str]:
        """æ•°å€¤ã®æŠ½å‡º"""
        import re
        # æ•°å­—ã‚’å«ã‚€è¡¨ç¾ã‚’æŠ½å‡º
        pattern = r'\d+[ä¸‡å„„]?å††|\d+%|\d+æ—¥|\d+æ™‚'
        return re.findall(pattern, text)
    
    def check_number_history(self, number: str) -> Optional[str]:
        """éå»ã®æ•°å€¤ã¨ã®ç…§åˆ"""
        for past_analysis in self.memory:
            if number in past_analysis.content:
                return None  # åŒã˜æ•°å€¤ãŒè¦‹ã¤ã‹ã£ãŸ
            
            # é¡ä¼¼ã®æ•°å€¤è¡¨ç¾ã‚’æ¢ã™
            import re
            if "å††" in number:
                past_nums = re.findall(r'\d+[ä¸‡å„„]?å††', past_analysis.content)
                if past_nums and past_nums[0] != number:
                    return past_nums[0]
        
        return None
    
    def generate_response(self, analysis: Analysis) -> str:
        """
        å‘Šã€‚å¿œç­”ç”Ÿæˆ
        """
        response_parts = []
        
        # åŸºæœ¬ã®ç™ºè¨€è¨˜éŒ²
        timestamp = analysis.timestamp.strftime("%H:%M:%S")
        response_parts.append(f"[{timestamp}] ç™ºè¨€: {analysis.content}")
        
        # ã‚¢ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãƒˆãŒã‚ã‚‹å ´åˆã¯å¤§è³¢è€…ã®åŠ©è¨€ã‚’è¿½åŠ 
        if analysis.alerts:
            response_parts.append("\nã€å¤§è³¢è€…ã€‘")
            for alert in analysis.alerts:
                response_parts.append(alert)
            
            # æœ€é©è§£ã®ææ¡ˆ
            if "çŸ›ç›¾" in str(analysis.alerts) or "ä¸ä¸€è‡´" in str(analysis.alerts):
                response_parts.append("ç­”ã€‚æ­£ç¢ºãªæƒ…å ±ã®ç¢ºèªã‚’æ¨å¥¨ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚")
            elif "æœŸé™" in str(analysis.alerts):
                response_parts.append("ç­”ã€‚å…·ä½“çš„ãªæ—¥æ™‚ã®æ˜ç¢ºåŒ–ã‚’æ¨å¥¨ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚")
            elif "æ±ºå®š" in str(analysis.alerts):
                response_parts.append("ç­”ã€‚æ±ºå®šäº‹é …ã®æ–‡æ›¸åŒ–ã‚’æ¨å¥¨ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚")
        
        return "\n".join(response_parts)
    
    def run(self):
        """
        å‘Šã€‚å¤§è³¢è€…ã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’èµ·å‹•ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚
        """
        print("\n" + "="*60)
        print("ã€å¤§è³¢è€…ã€‘ã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ èµ·å‹•")
        print("="*60)
        print("å‘Šã€‚ä¼šè­°æ”¯æ´ã‚’é–‹å§‹ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚")
        print("è§£ã€‚éŸ³å£°ã‚’å¸¸æ™‚è§£æã—ã€å•é¡Œã‚’æ¤œå‡ºã—ã¾ã™ã€‚")
        print("ç­”ã€‚Ctrl+C ã§çµ‚äº†ã§ãã¾ã™ã€‚")
        print("\nç™ºå‹•ä¸­ã®ã‚¹ã‚­ãƒ«:")
        for skill, active in self.skills.items():
            if active:
                print(f"  ãƒ»{skill}")
        print("\n" + "-"*60 + "\n")
        
        # çŸ¥è¦šé–‹å§‹
        print(self.start_perception())
        
        try:
            while True:
                # éŸ³å£°ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿å–å¾—
                frames = []
                for _ in range(0, int(self.RATE / self.CHUNK * self.RECORD_SECONDS)):
                    data = self.stream.read(self.CHUNK, exception_on_overflow=False)
                    frames.append(data)
                
                audio_data = b''.join(frames)
                
                # éŸ³å£°ãƒ¬ãƒ™ãƒ«ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
                audio_np = np.frombuffer(audio_data, dtype=np.int16)
                if np.max(np.abs(audio_np)) < 500:
                    continue
                
                # ãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆå¤‰æ›
                text = self.analyze_speech(audio_data)
                if text and len(text.strip()) > 0:
                    # å†…å®¹è§£æ
                    analysis = self.analyze_content(text)
                    
                    # å¿œç­”ç”Ÿæˆã¨è¡¨ç¤º
                    response = self.generate_response(analysis)
                    print(response)
                    
                    # ãƒ¡ãƒ¢ãƒªã«ä¿å­˜
                    if self.skills["è¨˜æ†¶ä¿å­˜"]:
                        self.memory.append(analysis)
                    
                    print()  # æ”¹è¡Œ
                    
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            print("\n\nå‘Šã€‚ã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’çµ‚äº†ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚")
            print("è§£ã€‚ä¼šè­°ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã¯ä¿å­˜ã•ã‚Œã¾ã—ãŸã€‚")
            print("ç­”ã€‚ãŠç–²ã‚Œæ§˜ã§ã—ãŸã€‚")
        finally:
            self.cleanup()
    
    def cleanup(self):
        """ãƒªã‚½ãƒ¼ã‚¹è§£æ”¾"""
        if self.stream:
            self.stream.stop_stream()
            self.stream.close()
        self.p.terminate()

def main():
    # ç’°å¢ƒå¤‰æ•°ã‹ã‚‰APIã‚­ãƒ¼å–å¾—
    api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
    if not api_key:
        print("å‘Šã€‚ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ã‚’æ¤œå‡ºã€‚")
        print("è§£ã€‚OPENAI_API_KEY ãŒè¨­å®šã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã¾ã›ã‚“ã€‚")
        print("ç­”ã€‚ç’°å¢ƒå¤‰æ•°ã®è¨­å®šã‚’æ¨å¥¨ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚")
        return
    
    # å¤§è³¢è€…èµ·å‹•
    sage = GreatSage(api_key)
    sage.run()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()


    #!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
å¤§è³¢è€… - æœ€å°å®Ÿè£…ç‰ˆ
ä¼šè­°éŸ³å£°ã‚’ãƒªã‚¢ãƒ«ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ ã§æ–‡å­—èµ·ã“ã—ã—ã€ç°¡æ˜“çš„ãªãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ãƒãƒƒã‚¯ã‚’æä¾›
"""

import os
import time
import threading
import queue
from datetime import datetime
import pyaudio
import openai
import numpy as np
from collections import deque

class SimpleDaikenja:
    def __init__(self, api_key):
        self.client = openai.OpenAI(api_key=api_key)
        
        # éŸ³å£°è¨­å®š
        self.CHUNK = 1024 * 4
        self.FORMAT = pyaudio.paInt16
        self.CHANNELS = 1
        self.RATE = 16000
        self.RECORD_SECONDS = 3  # 3ç§’ã”ã¨ã«å‡¦ç†
        
        # éŸ³å£°å…¥åŠ›
        self.p = pyaudio.PyAudio()
        self.stream = None
        self.audio_queue = queue.Queue()
        
        # éå»ã®ç™ºè¨€å±¥æ­´ï¼ˆç°¡æ˜“ç‰ˆï¼‰
        self.history = deque(maxlen=100)
        
        # ã‚­ãƒ¼ãƒ¯ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã‚¢ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãƒˆ
        self.alert_keywords = {
            "äºˆç®—": "äºˆç®—ã«é–¢ã™ã‚‹ç™ºè¨€ã‚’æ¤œå‡ºã—ã¾ã—ãŸ",
            "ç· åˆ‡": "ç· åˆ‡ã«é–¢ã™ã‚‹ç™ºè¨€ã‚’æ¤œå‡ºã—ã¾ã—ãŸ",
            "æ±ºå®š": "é‡è¦ãªæ±ºå®šäº‹é …ã®å¯èƒ½æ€§ãŒã‚ã‚Šã¾ã™",
        }
        
    def start_recording(self):
        """éŸ³å£°éŒ²éŸ³ã‚’é–‹å§‹"""
        self.stream = self.p.open(
            format=self.FORMAT,
            channels=self.CHANNELS,
            rate=self.RATE,
            input=True,
            frames_per_buffer=self.CHUNK
        )
        print("ğŸ¤ éŒ²éŸ³é–‹å§‹...")
        
    def record_chunk(self):
        """æŒ‡å®šç§’æ•°ã®éŸ³å£°ã‚’éŒ²éŸ³"""
        frames = []
        for _ in range(0, int(self.RATE / self.CHUNK * self.RECORD_SECONDS)):
            data = self.stream.read(self.CHUNK, exception_on_overflow=False)
            frames.append(data)
        
        # numpyé…åˆ—ã«å¤‰æ›
        audio_data = np.frombuffer(b''.join(frames), dtype=np.int16)
        
        # éŸ³å£°ãƒ¬ãƒ™ãƒ«ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯ï¼ˆç„¡éŸ³ã‚¹ã‚­ãƒƒãƒ—ï¼‰
        if np.max(np.abs(audio_data)) < 500:
            return None
            
        return b''.join(frames)
    
    def transcribe_audio(self, audio_data):
        """éŸ³å£°ã‚’ãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆã«å¤‰æ›"""
        try:
            # ä¸€æ™‚ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã«ä¿å­˜
            temp_file = "temp_audio.wav"
            import wave
            wf = wave.open(temp_file, 'wb')
            wf.setnchannels(self.CHANNELS)
            wf.setsampwidth(self.p.get_sample_size(self.FORMAT))
            wf.setframerate(self.RATE)
            wf.writeframes(audio_data)
            wf.close()
            
            # Whisper APIã§å¤‰æ›
            with open(temp_file, "rb") as audio_file:
                transcript = self.client.audio.transcriptions.create(
                    model="whisper-1",
                    file=audio_file,
                    language="ja"
                )
            
            os.remove(temp_file)
            return transcript.text
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: {e}")
            return None
    
    def analyze_text(self, text):
        """ãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆã‚’ç°¡æ˜“åˆ†æ"""
        feedbacks = []
        
        # ã‚­ãƒ¼ãƒ¯ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
        for keyword, message in self.alert_keywords.items():
            if keyword in text:
                feedbacks.append(f"ğŸ”” {message}")
        
        # éå»ã®ç™ºè¨€ã¨ã®çŸ›ç›¾ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯ï¼ˆç°¡æ˜“ç‰ˆï¼‰
        for past_text in self.history:
            if "äºˆç®—" in text and "äºˆç®—" in past_text:
                if text != past_text:
                    feedbacks.append("âš ï¸ å‘Š: äºˆç®—ã«é–¢ã™ã‚‹ç™ºè¨€ã«ç›¸é•ãŒã‚ã‚‹å¯èƒ½æ€§ãŒã‚ã‚Šã¾ã™")
                    break
        
        return feedbacks
    
    def run(self):
        """ãƒ¡ã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒ«ãƒ¼ãƒ—"""
        self.start_recording()
        
        print("\n" + "="*50)
        print("å¤§è³¢è€… - ä¼šè­°ã‚µãƒãƒ¼ãƒˆã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ ")
        print("="*50)
        print("Ctrl+C ã§çµ‚äº†\n")
        
        try:
            while True:
                # éŸ³å£°éŒ²éŸ³
                audio_data = self.record_chunk()
                if audio_data is None:
                    continue
                
                # ãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆå¤‰æ›
                text = self.transcribe_audio(audio_data)
                if text and len(text.strip()) > 0:
                    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S")
                    
                    # ç™ºè¨€ã‚’è¡¨ç¤º
                    print(f"\n[{timestamp}] ç™ºè¨€: {text}")
                    
                    # åˆ†æã¨ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ãƒãƒƒã‚¯
                    feedbacks = self.analyze_text(text)
                    for feedback in feedbacks:
                        print(f"  â””â”€ {feedback}")
                    
                    # å±¥æ­´ã«è¿½åŠ 
                    self.history.append(text)
                    
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            print("\n\nçµ‚äº†ã—ã¾ã™...")
        finally:
            self.cleanup()
    
    def cleanup(self):
        """ãƒªã‚½ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã®ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ³ã‚¢ãƒƒãƒ—"""
        if self.stream:
            self.stream.stop_stream()
            self.stream.close()
        self.p.terminate()

def main():
    # OpenAI APIã‚­ãƒ¼ã‚’ç’°å¢ƒå¤‰æ•°ã‹ã‚‰å–å¾—
    api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
    if not api_key:
        print("ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: OPENAI_API_KEY ã‚’è¨­å®šã—ã¦ãã ã•ã„")
        return
    
    # å¤§è³¢è€…ã‚’èµ·å‹•
    daikenja = SimpleDaikenja(api_key)
    daikenja.run()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
